FROM [Categories] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a0].[Name], [a].[Id], [a0].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[Category_Id]
    FROM [AnimalCategories] AS [a]
    LEFT JOIN [Animals] AS [a0] ON [a].[Animal_Id] = [a0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [c].[Id] = [t].[Category_Id]
ORDER BY [c].[Id], [t].[Id]
